{\footnotesize\ttfamily const P\+H\+P\+\_\+\+Q\+U\+E\+R\+Y\+\_\+\+R\+F\+C3986 2}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily const S\+ID \char`\"{}name=ID\char`\"{}}

(P\+H\+P4, P\+H\+P5) 

Constant containing either the session name and session ID in the form of \char`\"{}name=\+I\+D\char`\"{} or empty string if session ID was set in an appropriate session cookie. This is the same id as the one returned by \mbox{\hyperlink{session_8php_a75041e1e817ff34864ae2bdc3fe9e574}{session\+\_\+id()}}. \begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{STREAM\_MUST\_SEEK}{STREAM\_MUST\_SEEK}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily const S\+T\+R\+E\+A\+M\+\_\+\+M\+U\+S\+T\+\_\+\+S\+E\+EK 16}

This flag is useful when your extension really must be able to randomly seek around in a stream. Some streams may not be seekable in their native form, so this flag asks the streams A\+PI to check to see if the stream does support seeking. If it does not, it will copy the stream into temporary storage (which may be a temporary file or a memory stream) which does support seeking. Please note that this flag is not useful when you want to seek the stream and write to it, because the stream you are accessing might not be bound to the actual resource you requested. If the requested resource is network based, this flag will cause the opener to block until the whole contents have been downloaded. \mbox{\hyperlink{patch2_8txt_a3f9992ab8fa942ed02faa63682c3a84c}{https\+://php.\+net/manual/en/internals2.\+ze1.\+streams.\+constants.\+php}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{standard__defines_8php_ae4ace1f5107de3077d4932c6d6bf2ec5}\label{standard__defines_8php_ae4ace1f5107de3077d4932c6d6bf2ec5}} 
\index{standard\_defines.php@{standard\_defines.php}!STREAM\_NOTIFY\_AUTH\_REQUIRED@{STREAM\_NOTIFY\_AUTH\_REQUIRED}}
\index{STREAM\_NOTIFY\_AUTH\_REQUIRED@{STREAM\_NOTIFY\_AUTH\_REQUIRED}!standard\_defines.php@{standard\_defines.php}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{STREAM\_NOTIFY\_AUTH\_REQUIRED}{STREAM\_NOTIFY\_AUTH\_REQUIRED}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily const S\+T\+R\+E\+A\+M\+\_\+\+N\+O\+T\+I\+F\+Y\+\_\+\+A\+U\+T\+H\+\_\+\+R\+E\+Q\+U\+I\+R\+ED 3}

Additional authorization is required to access the specified resource. Typical issued with severity level of S\+T\+R\+E\+A\+M\+\_\+\+N\+O\+T\+I\+F\+Y\+\_\+\+S\+E\+V\+E\+R\+I\+T\+Y\+\_\+\+E\+RR. \mbox{\hyperlink{patch2_8txt_a3f9992ab8fa942ed02faa63682c3a84c}{https\+://php.\+net/manual/en/stream.\+constants.\+php}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{standard__defines_8php_aad78b9e9ce34dd412797dea1d78ee8c6}\label{standard__defines_8php_aad78b9e9ce34dd412797dea1d78ee8c6}}
